Lens

Image quality, image speed, sensor and noise level on the LENS sensor are measured by a series of sensors which measure the luminance of the light, the resolution of the image, white balance, gamma and other features of the image. When using the sensor to convert a picture to image ratio, the amount of white balance is calculated using the following formulas.
